  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0b4c5ee5-1503-403b-9ebf-ce84f7c992fb'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer11848141326543475777">When Mikayla imagined her prom night, she envisioned a fairy-tale evening full of romance. With no one to turn to, Mikayla is forced</span>
  <span id="freeText11848141326543475777" style="display:none">When Mikayla imagined her prom night, she envisioned a fairy-tale evening full of romance. So when betrayal and tragedy come in quick succession, Mikayla is completely destroyed. Suddenly, everything she loved and everyone she relied on are tragically, irrevocably gone.<br /><br />Jake, a handsome boy she just met, happens to witness her loss. With no one to turn to, Mikayla is forced to depend on this near stranger and his family, and he in turn is determined to take care of her. But Mikayla—thrust into adulthood with no one to guide her—is desperate to contain her grief and hide what she considers to be her weakness. Mikayla and Jake both want more, but despite their growing closeness and intense chemistry, she tries to keep her distance and protect her heart. As he does everything in his power to win her trust, Mikayla must choose between remaining alone and safe or letting love in.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/667764259?book_show_action=true">Jul 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer667764259" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18326700608418838688"><br/><b>5- <i>I more than a lot liked this book</i>- stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/b40e4fd5-21f0-4b53-9148-dac9ec388ff0_zpsf65fc7e6.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429199i/859543.jpg' alt=' photo b40e4fd5-21f0-4b53-9148-dac9ec388ff0_zpsf65fc7e6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This book hooked me from the start and I couldn’t put it down. Loved every single page! I’m going to throw this out at the very beginning of my review- this one is going straight to the favorites shelf! <br/><br/><b>In one night my fairytale ended... or it may have begun. </b> <br/>It’s just one day. 24 hours. But for Mikayla, that one day alters her entire life. Kayla’s life was pretty great. She had fun and awesome parents, a sweet little sister, a best friend- Mega</span>
  <span id="freeText18326700608418838688" style="display:none"><br><b>5- <i>I more than a lot liked this book</i>- stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/b40e4fd5-21f0-4b53-9148-dac9ec388ff0_zpsf65fc7e6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429199i/859543.jpg" alt=" photo b40e4fd5-21f0-4b53-9148-dac9ec388ff0_zpsf65fc7e6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book hooked me from the start and I couldn’t put it down. Loved every single page! I’m going to throw this out at the very beginning of my review- this one is going straight to the favorites shelf! <br><br><b>In one night my fairytale ended... or it may have begun. </b> <br>It’s just one day. 24 hours. But for Mikayla, that one day alters her entire life. Kayla’s life was pretty great. She had fun and awesome parents, a sweet little sister, a best friend- Megan, and her boyfriend of 4 years, James. In one night, she loses them all in some way. In that night, she also finds the other half of her heart. <br><br>Kayla meets Jake, the circumstances are less than ideal, but in some way or another, they just connect. She would never know this random guy she meets on the night of her prom will change her life, save her life. Jake doesn’t know what it is about Mikayla, but from the moment he lays eyes on her, he knows. Something is different about this girl. He can’t let her walk away. <br><br>After a traumatic event, Kayla finds herself leaning on Jake, relying on Jake, this boy she has known less than 24 hours makes her feel safe, cared for, he lessens the pain.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/82432699-52a6-485a-b2da-80c770f0012e_zps4d65867c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429199i/859544.jpg" alt=" photo 82432699-52a6-485a-b2da-80c770f0012e_zps4d65867c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Their bond, their friendship, it’s just amazing. <b>JAKE</b> is just amazing. I’m talking Josh Bennett, Andrew Parrish type amazing. The best kind. I’m a little obsessed with this guy. As time goes on, Jake and his family and friends are exactly what Kayla needs to heal and try to get on with her life. She and Jake have some serious feelings for each other, even if they don’t admit them out loud. Jake gives Kayla the strength she needs to go on. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I think I’m in love with this beautifully broken girl.</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/34207d56-6120-43ea-a22e-7f9cf82f7ebc_zps536bcf6a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429199i/859545.jpg" alt=" photo 34207d56-6120-43ea-a22e-7f9cf82f7ebc_zps536bcf6a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>I so much more than a lot like you.</blockquote>
</b><br>I loved the friendship these two developed. The intimate moments they shared. The build up and sexual tension was off the charts. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/6574a39e-a326-4d9a-ab5d-be8033371ec3_zps06caf12b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429199i/859546.jpg" alt=" photo 6574a39e-a326-4d9a-ab5d-be8033371ec3_zps06caf12b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Waiting for these two to reveal how they truly felt for one another was brutal at times... even though they weren’t official, I loved that they still belonged to each other. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/16506ee6-6756-4a9b-8ea3-af6b5f74ab46_zpsae04032a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429199i/859547.jpg" alt=" photo 16506ee6-6756-4a9b-8ea3-af6b5f74ab46_zpsae04032a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>All Jake ever wanted was to be there for Kayla, to take care of her, love her. But he wants all of her, not just parts, so he waits until she is ready to give him all of it. <br><b>
  <blockquote>It’s the fucking hardest thing to do, to be around the person you love, with everything you have, and not be able to love them.</blockquote>
</b><br>Kayla knows how she feels about Jake. She has never doubted those feelings. Others can see it too...<br><b>
  <blockquote>The way she looks at you- like you’re the only one. You’re it, Jake. You’re all of it. Her forever.</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/8068db57-383c-4f12-b8e5-b36810a276ad_zps42fd3fdb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429199i/859548.jpg" alt=" photo 8068db57-383c-4f12-b8e5-b36810a276ad_zps42fd3fdb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>‘It’s just you. It’s only ever been just you. It will always only ever be just you.’</blockquote>
</b><br>It’s just getting to the point in her life when Kayla feels complete enough to be with Jake wholly that is difficult. But sometimes, you have to move on. Let go. Embrace your life. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I will not let bad people dictate what should be a good life.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Some of my FAVORITE things/quotes:<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/6aff0df5-7417-49d5-95ff-8baba46255e9_zps22983bd4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429199i/859549.jpg" alt=" photo 6aff0df5-7417-49d5-95ff-8baba46255e9_zps22983bd4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>‘Why does he get to call you Kayla, and everyone else calls you Mickey?’ I shrug. ‘Because my family called me Kayla.’<br><br>Do not settle for anything less that the Jake Andrews of the world. Because they exist, and not just in fairytales.<br><br>Once he’s inside me, I work it out, why I never felt like this before. Because if I compare my feelings for Jake to anyone else, then I know. I know I’ve never loved anyone before. Not even a little bit. Not even at all.<br><br>I love him, so much more than a lot. </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>This book was just all kinds of awesome. It will put you through the ringer emotionally. The best part was, even through all the tears and devastating, emotional moments, there were a lot of smiles, a lot of swooning, and a lot of laughter. Isn’t that the best kind of book? That can make you feel, make you cry, but also makes you happy. It is for me. I loved the dual pov- inside of Jakes head... YES! I know I touched on this a little bit before, but Jake Andrews... Jake was everything you could ever want in a man. Seriously the best. Without him, I don’t even know how Kayla’s story would have turned out. He is just incredible! There were also some pretty wonderful secondary characters: Lucy and Logan were my favorite. I swear Lucy could be my twin- lol ;) And Logan... I am so happy he is getting his own book. But the ending sentence or two... what was that? I need more of this guy! <br><br>Heartbreaking, heartwarming, beautiful and emotional story about love, friendship, moving on and letting go. Don’t pass this one up. I can’t even tell you why I loved it so much- it just gave me that ‘feeling’, you know, the one you get after you read a book you can’t get out of your head- I just was so happy after reading, you couldn’t get that smile off of my face! Highly recommend this one!!! ♥</span>
  <a data-text-id="18326700608418838688" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer661614271" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1357607752883808125">SPOILER FREE REVIEW -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br/>5 STARS out of 5<br/>Genre:New Adult Romance<br/>2013 FAVORITE<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380375136ra/729624.gif' alt=' photo hearts_zps2cbeef3d.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>That moment when you find a book you love..and can barely contain your excitement because you want to share it with EVERY ONE<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428312ra/856938.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_men8o9eWHt1r4hu81_zps7388a7f9.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>It can’t be just me… You have to read this book I cannot be alone in this love fest. I need my fellow book lovers to read this book! ASAP!<br/><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>My Casting</u>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428312i/856939.jpg' alt=' photo 95664ae6-976e-494f-b104-bccc3c537c46_zps1ce47802.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>REVIEW</b><br/><br/><b>Because I need to know.<br/>I need to know how she feels and what she wants from me, from this.<br/> If she wa</b></span>
  <span id="freeText1357607752883808125" style="display:none">SPOILER FREE REVIEW -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br>5 STARS out of 5<br>Genre:New Adult Romance<br>2013 FAVORITE<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380375136ra/729624.gif" alt=" photo hearts_zps2cbeef3d.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That moment when you find a book you love..and can barely contain your excitement because you want to share it with EVERY ONE<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428312ra/856938.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_men8o9eWHt1r4hu81_zps7388a7f9.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>It can’t be just me… You have to read this book I cannot be alone in this love fest. I need my fellow book lovers to read this book! ASAP!<br><br><br><br><b>
  <u>My Casting</u>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428312i/856939.jpg" alt=" photo 95664ae6-976e-494f-b104-bccc3c537c46_zps1ce47802.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>REVIEW</b><br><br><b>Because I need to know.<br>I need to know how she feels and what she wants from me, from this.<br> If she wants to be <i>MORE THAN THIS</i>.</b> ~Jake<br><br>Prom night should be one of the best nights of your teen life right? Well, that is not the case for Mikayla. For her prom night becomes the night her life forever changed; in more ways than one.<br><br><i>
  <b>‘I look over at the cute brunette and wait for a reaction. I feel like I should leave, like what I’m witnessing is too intimate, too personal. But my feet are locked to the floor. I have no idea why, but I can’t look away. <br>I can’t walk away.’</b>
</i> ~Jake<br><br>Jake and Mikayla meet under horribly embarrassing circumstances, nevertheless they bond and by the end of the night whether they realize it or not they are tied to each other for life.<br><br>I spent the beginning of this book an emotional wreck. <br>At 3% I was steaming mad. <br>At 14% I was happy and laughing my ass off. <br>At 17% I get hit right in the back of my head with a sledge hammer. It hurt…It hurt so damn bad.<br><br>As Mikayla tries to reassemble the pieces of her life that are left she becomes close to Jake and his family. A guy who barely knows her but now holds her fragile heart in his hands. Moving on is not easy yet she slowly does and Jake is right by her side. Mikayla quickly learns that Jake is,<i> The Jake Andrews,</i> an all star baseball pitcher and predicted to go pro.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/629863.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mfyxwv8uEN1s24qdco1_500_zps92213652.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/629866.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mfyxonbE3y1s24qdco1_500_zps01858c38.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>A very close friendship blooms between them; at times it is so intimate that I felt like I was intruding on all the moments they would share. Jake is careful not to push her in to something she is not ready for. But he wants her. B A D. Not just sex either. He wants her. All of her.<br><br><b>And she wants him too. All of him.</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428312i/856940.jpg" alt=" photo c494b376-5632-48d6-a5d8-c540f26881eb_zps7838d601.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428312i/856941.jpg" alt=" photo 12bbd4f9-dc1e-4161-8f13-230aa876b051_zps939059f8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380428312i/856942.jpg" alt=" photo 7f80309e-d1c9-456e-b938-9c6e824afe09_zpsa3b46885.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The intensely burning chemistry with these two makes for some very steamy angst filled moments!<br><br><b>
  <i>‘Nothing like a mind blowing orgasm to keep a goofy smile on my face. <br>Oh. <br>My. <br>God. <br>Jake. <br>Fucking. <br>Andrews.’</i>
</b> ~Mikayla<br><br><i>
  <b>‘We’re looking so intently into each others eyes, trying to see into each others souls. <br>Talking without speaking. <br>Feeling without touching.’</b>
</i> ~Mikayla <br><br><i>
  <b>‘I’m two seconds away from exploding and I warn her but she won’t. fucking. stop.’ </b>
</i> ~Jake<br><br><b>
  <i>‘He kisses away the tears that have fallen all over my wet face. Then he looks at me, really looks at me. And then his lips are on mine, and my eyes close because the sensation is so overpowering.’</i>
</b> ~ Mikayla<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428312ra/856943.gif" alt=" photo fanning_my_vagina_zps869c36e8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>
  <b>Fave scenes</b>
</u>(without any major details)<br><br><b>-After prom the bon fire...<br><br>-Every scene with Logan...<br><br>-The letters...<br><br>-The Prince in a Flashback of a young Mikayla being told a story by her mom...</b><br><br><u>My Thoughts</u><br>The story is told in dual pov so we get inside both Jake and Mikayla’s head which I must say is a true pleasure. READ THIS BOOK! You know you’ve struck gold when a book can make you<br>Happy, sad, laugh out loud, swoon, then cry all in the first 20% of reading.<br><u>The characters</u> <b>Jake</b> is a total alpha. You best not look and you sure as hell better not touch his girl because he won’t hesitate to whoop that ass. He is also loving, tender, sweet, understanding and patient with Mikayla. It is as if he was exactly what she needed and vice versa. And yeah, he’s kind of a big deal! <br><b>Mikayla</b> this girl goes through so much yet she is still standing talk about recovering from a lost. After losing so much you can barely breathe. She is just..WOW. Smart, funny and no idea how beautiful she is, inside and out!<br>I gave these two a pass for not being able to communicate all of their feelings. Which can be frustrating for readers. They are both 18, so I feel as though characters under age 22 get passes because they most likely have not had the chance to be in more than 1 long term relationship yet. Even with my pass they fared well. Insecurity was the biggest issue with these two.<br><br><u>The secondary characters</u> will not only catch your attention, they will leave you wanting more. Mainly Logan, the guy is freaking hilarious. I think for me the best part of the secondary character roles are played by the parents. The parents carry a strong presence in this book. Major thumbs up for that Jay McLean!<br><br>Dear Megan,<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/677103.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mnmeprA33S1qz4rgp_zpsa3d2ab4c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428312ra/856944.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mhz57oC0sM1r721d2o1_500_zps96b1c84b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>The ending,</u> no cliffhanger… BUT even though we get a sweet epilogue, readers will still get a nice little twist at the end. This twist will leave your jaw on the ground. Trust me. Because even though you could have predicted it… So much goes down in the book that you forget about it until its right in front of your face on the page. It is literally the last sentence of the book...<br><br><br>My Ratings<br>Characters- lovable, witty and charming<br>Writing Style- Fair, there was excessive usage of slang and a few editing issues<br>Plot/Storyline- Strong it will grab you from the first page<br>Steam Factor- High/VERY HOT<br>Overall- I LOVED IT! READ IT!!!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br>For more reviews got to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a><br><b>*Copy kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review*</b></span>

<div id="review_1552418622" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1552418622" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1552418622?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=biggest-dissapointment">biggest-dissapointment</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1552418622" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8038442611969248171"><u>
  <b>(SPOILERS ahead...)</b>
</u><br/><br/>It took every ounce of control I had not to DNF this book. It's one of the most <b>unrealistic</b> stories I've ever come across with!<br/><br/>Here are the reasons why I didn't like it:<br/><br/><b>UNREALISTIC PLOT</b> - This is a work of fiction, I know. But why make the whole thing unbelievable to the extreme? <b>Mikayla</b> found out one day that her boyfriend cheated on her with her best friend. That same day, she also met the gorgeous guy with a sexy Aussie accent named <b>Jake</b> and well, instantly felt attract</span>
  <span id="freeText8038442611969248171" style="display:none"><u>
  <b>(SPOILERS ahead...)</b>
</u><br><br>It took every ounce of control I had not to DNF this book. It's one of the most <b>unrealistic</b> stories I've ever come across with!<br><br>Here are the reasons why I didn't like it:<br><br><b>UNREALISTIC PLOT</b> - This is a work of fiction, I know. But why make the whole thing unbelievable to the extreme? <b>Mikayla</b> found out one day that her boyfriend cheated on her with her best friend. That same day, she also met the gorgeous guy with a sexy Aussie accent named <b>Jake</b> and well, instantly felt attracted to him. THAT VERY SAME DAY, she experienced great loss when her family members were murdered. The next day, she became part of Jake's family and Jake's family offered her shelter even if she's a complete stranger. Okay, I don't mean to sound so selfish and insensitive here because the girl lost everything she had, but honestly, all shit happened in one day? <br><br><b>MIKAYLA</b> - Mikayla is also one of those unbelievable heroines ever existed. She just lost everything but I couldn't believe her way of coping. It didn't take her a week to move on. She can even laugh with Jake's friends and she even had time to entertain such unnecessary thoughts.. like how Jake is so damn sexy and how his accent always gets her and so forth and so on. <br><br><b>INSTA-LOVE </b> - YES. Insta-love big time!!!<br><br><b>SIDE CHARACTERS</b> - Why everyone that is close to Jake treats Mikayla like the way they treat an old-time friend confuses me. How did these people instantly warm up to her? They've just met her and then, just like that? So unbelievable!<br><br><b>TOO MUCH JEALOUSY AND INSECURITIES ALL OVER THE PLACE</b> - Nuff said. <br><br>I cannot bring myself to recommend this book to others because it's completely <b>over-the-top </b>. Much as I tried, I just couldn't like this book. I was groaning inwardly and rolling my eyes at every scene. Ugh. Overall, this book wasn't for me. I didn't feel connected to everything. <br><br>Rating:<br><br>1 Star<br><br><p>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

      Jacqueline and Hazel
  </div>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1181931915" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2023424630937469608"><b>4.5 STARS</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/10580000_1552483881630576_7906209586430500688_n_zpssxtmhgaa.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424828205i/13806620._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo 10580000_1552483881630576_7906209586430500688_n_zpssxtmhgaa.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>More Than This is book one in the More Than series by Jay McLean. This book was recommended to me by two different friends but I hadn’t really read many reviews so it took me by completely by surprise. I WAS NOT prepared for all the feels, and let me tell you, there are plenty. And the hotness factor, oh my gosh, was off the charts. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_nf5kfnv3uw1rkt3l4o1_500_zpsc9i9z4b9.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424828205i/13806621.jpg' alt=' photo tumblr_nf5kfnv3uw1rkt3l4o1_500_zpsc9i9z4b9.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Mikayla is eighteen years old, just two weeks away from graduation, and it’s prom night. She is going with her boyfriend of four years, James, and h</span>
  <span id="freeText2023424630937469608" style="display:none"><b>4.5 STARS</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/10580000_1552483881630576_7906209586430500688_n_zpssxtmhgaa.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424828205i/13806620._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 10580000_1552483881630576_7906209586430500688_n_zpssxtmhgaa.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>More Than This is book one in the More Than series by Jay McLean. This book was recommended to me by two different friends but I hadn’t really read many reviews so it took me by completely by surprise. I WAS NOT prepared for all the feels, and let me tell you, there are plenty. And the hotness factor, oh my gosh, was off the charts. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_nf5kfnv3uw1rkt3l4o1_500_zpsc9i9z4b9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424828205i/13806621.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_nf5kfnv3uw1rkt3l4o1_500_zpsc9i9z4b9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Mikayla is eighteen years old, just two weeks away from graduation, and it’s prom night. She is going with her boyfriend of four years, James, and her best friend, Megan. Mikayla has a wonderful family, her parents and little sister. She and James have their college all picked out and everything is perfect. This night is going to be perfect…or so she thought. <br><br>The night that started out with so much promise ended up being the night that forever changed her life, her future. It was a night of betrayal and horror. That is also the night she met Jake.<br><br><b>
  <i>“How can everything, EVERYTHING, be taken from me instantly?”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/baseball-pitcher_zpsc16a7f5c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419991246i/13152913.jpg" alt=" photo baseball-pitcher_zpsc16a7f5c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jake is also eighteen years old. He is a star pitcher and as his parents would say, kind of a big deal. His college scholarship is in place, his future set. He just happened to be at the same restaurant as Mikayla that night, Jake with his own friends, when he witnessed the beginning of the downfall of Mikayla’s night. So like her very own prince charming, he rescued her. He introduced her to his friends who accepted her immediately as one of the group. Little did they know what the rest of the evening had in store for them.<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_m1nnbkkN8I1rsddxho1_500_zpsc036fda9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415931210i/11867250.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_m1nnbkkN8I1rsddxho1_500_zpsc036fda9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After the horrors of that night, Jake’s family takes her in and Jake is by her side every step of the way. He is her strength, her rock. She can’t stand to be away from him for even a minute. As the days and weeks progress, their bond strengthens. <br><br><b>
  <i>“She’s just, more, than anyone else. We haven’t slept together, we haven’t even kissed, and she’s just…more.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_nju1xb889O1rarw77o1_500_zpsn6yqleyz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424828205i/13806622.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_nju1xb889O1rarw77o1_500_zpsn6yqleyz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book is full of the healing power of love. Jake’s family and friends take Kayla in as one of their own, never hesitating. Jake is patient, never asking more of her than she is willing to share. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Hey, Jake”<br>“Yeah, Kayla?” He’s almost asleep.<br>“I more than a lot like you.” It’s quiet for so long I don’t know if he heard me.<br>Then, “I more than a lot like you too, so much more than a lot.”</i>
</b><br><br>Jake knows he is in love with Kayla but he can’t tell her, not yet. He’s afraid she’s not ready to hear it, or what if she doesn’t feel the same way. Kayla knows she is in love with Jake as well. But she’s broken. How can she give herself to him when she’s broken? <br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m scared. So scared. That I won’t be enough. And that I’ll never really have him. My Jake.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/13667975403_zpsimckrcgc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424828205i/13806623.jpg" alt=" photo 13667975403_zpsimckrcgc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>These two were only eighteen years old but forced to deal with things that no adult should ever be faced with. But this book was really a story of the healing power of love. Jake, his family and his friends all giving Mikayla the love and strength she needs to get through the most difficult of times. This book is full of so many fantastic quotes. The chemistry between these two freaking electric. And wow, the ending. That was a shocker. Well, two shockers actually. The author knows just how to make us want to come back and read the next book. It worked because now I’m hooked and will have to continue on with book two, More Than Her, and get Logan’s story.<br><br><b>
  <i>“It’s just you. It’s only ever been just you. It will always only ever be just you.”</i>
</b> <br></span>

<div id="review_668419152" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/668419152" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/668419152?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18129149-more-than-this">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer668419152" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8760866247764324477"><b>*3 Stars*</b><br/><br/>Great story, but left me slightly conflicted...<br/><br/>This book had such a <b>powerful</b>, gripping start that broke my heart and made me anxious for the complex story I presumed would follow. Instead, I found that the middle strayed considerably from the intensity and intrigue of its promising beginning. That's not to say that I didn't enjoy what this story offered, because I did. But I felt some major issues were never fully explored while certain trivial issues were intensified. Luckily, the endi</span>
  <span id="freeText8760866247764324477" style="display:none"><b>*3 Stars*</b><br><br>Great story, but left me slightly conflicted...<br><br>This book had such a <b>powerful</b>, gripping start that broke my heart and made me anxious for the complex story I presumed would follow. Instead, I found that the middle strayed considerably from the intensity and intrigue of its promising beginning. That's not to say that I didn't enjoy what this story offered, because I did. But I felt some major issues were never fully explored while certain trivial issues were intensified. Luckily, the ending delivered some more of that awesomeness I was longing for!<br><br><i>More Than This</i> kicks off to a highly intense start: We are introduced to <b>Mikayla</b>, who is having a pretty crappy prom night, only to learn than things will shortly go from bad to worse. Or, more accurately, from bad to utterly <i>devastating</i>...<br><br><b>And. I. Was. Floored. </b><br><br>But, even in the midst of a world shattering tragedy, Makayla was granted a silver lining, and his name was <b>Jake Andrews</b>.<br><br>Jake quickly became Kayla's rock, and an undefined but intense relationship was formed. This is where the plot started to lose me a bit...<br><br>The ever popular jealousy and mistrust issues were a nice source of tension, at first, but then the book began to flood with it; until it was page after page of <i>'why are you talking to that guy; why is that girl staring at you?'</i> little conundrums. In moderation, this would have worked wonders. But it became far too consuming and began to downplay the original depth of the plot.<br><br>That said, there were really terrific elements that persuaded me to hang on to this story. The strong family/friendship dynamic was heartwarming and I loved that each character displayed their own personal redemption. There were many laugh-out-loud moments, and the characters were well-developed and extremely hard NOT to love! Jake and Kayla had an amazing, solid connection, even if they were hesitant to define it. <br><br>Jake was like an undercover alpha. He was sweet, caring, warm...and then <b>BAM! </b>Jake unleashes his possessive, dominant side that was both highly sexy and slightly bewildering. I thought maybe he'd have a sort of back story explaining his insecurities and extreme mood shifts, but I guess he just had a fun little caveman side. However, he was a true sweetheart and an amazingly sexy hero!<br><br>Although this story did sometimes yoyo my emotions, overall, it was a great read with beautiful messages of pain, healing, friendship, and love. Its concept was refreshing and unique, and I'm looking forward to Logan's story! <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Romance/New Adult<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> High. Very steamy!<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Intense and healing. Reluctant. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Sexy, possessive, and sweet hero. Damaged, funny, lovable heroine. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Shifted focus at times, but an overall solid, emotional execution. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Engaging, humorous, and intense. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person: Alternating dual perspectives. <br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None<br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> Character spinoff (Logan) <br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1183682587" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1183682587" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8429172-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595453256p2/8429172.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1183682587?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/8429172-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=dont-like-the-mcs-but-ugh">dont-like-the-mcs-but-ugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1183682587" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9625677032985162407">In the beginning I was having a fair amount of fun. I always enjoy contemporary reads and people had been recommending this series for a while now. Logan and Lucy's books in particular so those are the ones I'm anticipating the most.<br/><br/>I really tried to like this book and for a moment I thought I was going to but the characterization was so poor. There was no arc at all, either.<br/><br/>I was legit concerned about Mikayla's mental health because that girl did not mourn whatsoever. I'm not saying she had to </span>
  <span id="freeText9625677032985162407" style="display:none">In the beginning I was having a fair amount of fun. I always enjoy contemporary reads and people had been recommending this series for a while now. Logan and Lucy's books in particular so those are the ones I'm anticipating the most.<br /><br />I really tried to like this book and for a moment I thought I was going to but the characterization was so poor. There was no arc at all, either.<br /><br />I was legit concerned about Mikayla's mental health because that girl did not mourn whatsoever. I'm not saying she had to be crying on bed but can we all agree on the fact that she bottled up everything and just carried on with Jake's drama. No one ever even suggested her to go see a therapist and while Jake and his family and friends were there for her, Mikayla had a life before Jake and she supposedly had friends but she was left alone by almost everyone.<br /><br />I remember this trope that is, mostly, popular in contemporary romance books where the female lead leaves her life behind in order to adapt to her counterpart because suddenly all of her friends were fake or she did not have any. No relatives, nothing; and that's exactly what happened here just that in this case Mikayla's family was murdered and she doesn't do anything more than space out sometimes and that's it, because when Mikayla thinks about her family, it's always from Jake's POV so we don't have the process of grieving, accepting and moving on while honoring them.<br /><br />The only time we see Mikayla dealing with her family's death in a healthy way was on Emily's birthday and that part was nice but even then a lot of it revolved around Jake.<br /><br />It seems like I'm nitpicking and maybe I am but there was no depth to the main characters. I mean, we don't even know how they are adjusting to college life and how their classes go and if they have made new friends and work because that is never discussed. I don't know what kind of shit Mikayla and Jake even like. <br /><br />I enjoyed the last few chapters of the book more than the rest of it but ffs, I hated all that name calling and how Jake and Mikayla could not even stand other people around the other without getting sick with jealousy and it was so fucking stupid, I almost close the book several times. I swear, if I read slut, tramp and bitch one more time, I was going to have a stroke.<br /><br />Anyway, I hope the series get better as it goes because I did not like these one dimensional characters with only two personality traits: horny and jealous.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9625677032985162407" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I mean you can come to mine? I have a spare ticket and it would be a shame to waste a ticket and it would be a shame to waste that amazing dress. You look beautiful by the way. I’m swear I’m not a pyscho,” he continues… Look, I just don’t think you should let bad people dictate what should be a good time. Come hang out with me and my friends.”</i>
</b> <br><br>Then for a fair amount of scenes hanging out with Jake’s friends, Logan, Cam, Heidi, Lucy and Dylan. <br>I was a bit like… <br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/more%20than%20this/ilikeit_zpsc2d49153.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429376ra/860078.gif" alt=" photo ilikeit_zpsc2d49153.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/more%20than%20this/champagneyeah_zpsec766dde.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429376ra/860079.gif" alt=" photo champagneyeah_zpsec766dde.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429376ra/860080.gif" alt=" photo omg_zps69531d45.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>”Hi Mikayla. It’s nice to meet you,” she says quietly, then resumes reading. I look over at Cameron who just shrugs. “She’s on the last few chapters of some book she’s reading. She can’t stay away from it. We’re used to it now, we always find her reading at the oddest times. <br>I smile at Lucy. “What are you reading?” <br>She looks up at me and blushes a little, um, it’s called the Sea of Tranquilty,” it’s by – “ <br>“Josh Bennett, right?” </i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/more%20than%20this/BBF_zpsbfb10b9c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429376ra/860081.gif" alt=" photo BBF_zpsbfb10b9c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But then…. <br><br>Well then…. <br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/more%20than%20this/jayshocked_zps16cace7d.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429376ra/860082.gif" alt=" photo jayshocked_zps16cace7d.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “I know it’s too strange, and I know it might be circumstantial. Like we shared and experience and that somehow made us closer, but Lisa,” Kayla looks up at us now… “Jake, he makes things hurt a little less. He.. he’s home for me right now.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/beautiful%20lie%20reactions/grosssobbing_zps5d88337c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/more%20than%20this/screaming_zpsa9ffb25c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429376ra/860084.gif" alt=" photo screaming_zpsa9ffb25c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>And although you’re fucking heart is ripped out of your body! <br>Jake Andrews is A-FUCKIN-MAZING! <br><br>You swoon… Totally swoon… <br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/more%20than%20this/swoonfaint_zps8ef03228.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429376ra/860085.gif" alt=" photo swoonfaint_zps8ef03228.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> He’s not the hearts and flowers kind of guy, but he’s the heart and soul kind, and fuck if every girl would rather that then flowers.</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/more%20than%20this/stay_zps631b9c03.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429376ra/860087.gif" alt=" photo amazeballs_zpsfc07d051.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“Hey Jake?” <br>“Yeah Kayla?” He’s almost asleep. <br>“I more than a lot like you.” <br>It’s quiet for so long I don’t know if he heard me.<br>Then, “I more than a lot like you too, so much more than a lot.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/more%20than%20this/ST_zpsb5926c37.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Then James shows up again<br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/more%20than%20this/implied-facepalm_zps2613b369.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429376i/860089._SX540_.png" alt=" photo implied-facepalm_zps2613b369.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But then we are back to Jake! <br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/more%20than%20this/waving_zps3aa6bda2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429376ra/860090.gif" alt=" photo waving_zps3aa6bda2.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> It feels so intimate, like we’re more than what we are. I know I want to be. I want to be more than this.</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/more%20than%20this/Heshot_zps4918c3cc.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <i> Nothing says awkward like coming in your pants while dry humping.</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/more%20than%20this/hugs_zps4865a226.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>
  <i>We’re testing each other. Seeing how far we can take this before something snaps. Most likely my dick.</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/more%20than%20this/nowimhurt_zps473da552.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <i> “Jake, I can’t, I can’t be more than this, not now, not yet.”</i>

A LOT OF SHIT HAPPENS IN THIS BOOK!!! <br><br>And you will be annoyed with sexual tension….but it just makes it better… makes it more…. <br></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1226254966" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15806976072924804934">Find all of my reviews at: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/'>http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br/><br/>I was going to call this one “Hey, I just met you . . . and this is crazy, but my family just croaked so I’m going to move in to your house and have a completely unhealthy relationship with you maybe,” but I decided to go with something a little classier instead . . . <br/><br/><b>
  <i> “Nothing says awkward like coming in your pants while dry humping.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>If you’re only interested in the Cliff’s Notes version, here it is . . .<br/><br/><a href='http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426343656ra/14003985.gif' alt='Commercial Photography' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>The long version is Mi</span>
  <span id="freeText15806976072924804934" style="display:none">Find all of my reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/">http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br><br>I was going to call this one “Hey, I just met you . . . and this is crazy, but my family just croaked so I’m going to move in to your house and have a completely unhealthy relationship with you maybe,” but I decided to go with something a little classier instead . . . <br><br><b>
  <i> “Nothing says awkward like coming in your pants while dry humping.”</i>
</b><br><br>If you’re only interested in the Cliff’s Notes version, here it is . . .<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426343656ra/14003985.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The long version is Mikayla has been dating her high school boyfriend for four years. During her prom she discovers that her best friend has been banging him on the side for two of those years. Along comes Jake, a boy from another school with a smexy accent and a hero complex who decides to whisk her away to his own prom for the evening. Pretty crap night, huh? Ha! You ain't seen nuttin' yet. When Jake returns Mikayla home from their magical evening she discovers her entire family has been murdered . . . annnnnnnnd her house was set on fire by the perp, rendering her homeless. Jake once again saves the day and takes her home to his family in order to begin their extremely unhealthy instalovey love affair. It is there Kayla can become the most terrifying predator of all . . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426343656ra/14003986.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>and Jake can become a psycho who doesn't like "his girl" talking to - well, pretty much anyone at all . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426343656ra/14003987.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>We spend the next <s>gazillion</s> 250 or so pages dealing with the budding romance of the girl who has never experienced an "O Face" and the boy who brings it to her - via an epic bout of dry humping . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426343656ra/14003988.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Yeah. Even though these books are supposedly for adults, these two couldn't <i>possibly</i> do more than dry hump and fingerbang until nearly the last page and some "fade to black" sex. Seriously? Holy blue balls! How old are the people who write these books? Have they ever even seen a boy naked???? Talk about the unsexiest of sexytimes . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426343656ra/14003989.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Not to mention the fact that any girl/woman who calls her ladygarden the “down there” is not mature enough to be "doing it" in the first place.<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426343656ra/14003990.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>EDIT: This turd has a <b>4.23</b> rating?!?!?!?!<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">

      <a href="/user/show/2728874-c-money">C-Money</a>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9350753617088352697"><b>JUST ADDED Author Interview - > <a href='http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/2013/10/giveaway-book-review-more-than-this-by.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>HERE</a></b><br/><br/><b>SUPER ADORABLE character interview here - > <a href='http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jacqueline's Reads</a></b><br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/yhUlmOb' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><br/><b>5 STARS</b><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I more than a lot like you ... so much more than a lot</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/><br/>WHERE DO I BEGIN?! I'm just going to be upfront with you. I.LOVED.LOVED.LOVED.LOVED --- > MORE THAN THIS! <br/><br/><br/><blockquote>
<br/><b>My Emotions:</b><br/><br/><br/>At 1% - I had no idea what to expect, my girlfriend recommend it to me, so I said, oh what the heck.<br/><br/>At 1.1% - I KNEW this was going to be something special<br/><br/>At 8% I am grinning because of all the cuteness!<br/><br/>At </blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText9350753617088352697" style="display:none"><b>JUST ADDED Author Interview - &gt; <a href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/2013/10/giveaway-book-review-more-than-this-by.html" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a></b><br><br><b>SUPER ADORABLE character interview here - &gt; <a href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Jacqueline's Reads</a></b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/yhUlmOb" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430518i/863141._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>5 STARS</b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I more than a lot like you ... so much more than a lot</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><br>WHERE DO I BEGIN?! I'm just going to be upfront with you. I.LOVED.LOVED.LOVED.LOVED --- &gt; MORE THAN THIS! <br><br><br><blockquote>
<br><b>My Emotions:</b><br><br><br>At 1% - I had no idea what to expect, my girlfriend recommend it to me, so I said, oh what the heck.<br><br>At 1.1% - I KNEW this was going to be something special<br><br>At 8% I am grinning because of all the cuteness!<br><br>At 14% I am in a fit of laughter<br><br>At 17% I am like NOOOOO!!!!!! <br><br>At 38% I am shaking because I love it so much<br><br>At 82% I am crying big fat ugly tears<br><br>At 100% I had a book orgasm<br><br>YES.IT.WAS.THAT.GOOD</blockquote><br><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/42wvBXZ" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430518i/863142._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>It all begins with one night.... </b><br><br><br>Mikayla catches her boyfriend cheating on her with Mikayla's best friend on prom night. What an asshole right? Well, Jake was at the right place at the right time and suggests Mikayla spend prom night with him and his friends. Mikayla agrees.<br><br><br>The whole read was perfection and I really loved the beginning. I thought Mikayla (Kayla) and Jake had an adorable meet-cute. I am ALL about the damsel in distress story line, so this worked for me. The first 20% is really funny and will bring a smile to your face. I loved Jake's friends and the McLean wrote some fantastic side characters. I LOVED every single one of them from Cam, Lucy, Heidi, Dylan and Logan. Lucy is my favorite.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>We should totally be book best friends</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/hWARwhc" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430518i/863143.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Then the read shifts and you are just gutted. I wasn't expecting it and I was thinking to myself, oh lord, this is something, but it's also fantastic at the same time. Because of the shift Kayla and Jake become closer. I LOVED this. I thought Kayla and Jake were perfectly written characters. I loved Kayla. I thought she was just this sad broken, but beautiful and you couldn't help, but just-want-to-hug-her kind of girl. And Jake, LORD, how I love Jake. He is the alpha male we girls dream up, he's caring, yet possessive, aggressive and loyal. <br><br><br><b>Jake = Book Boyfriend.</b><br><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/e5c3HMV" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430518i/863144.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/NoZRGjU" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430518i/863145.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Oh and the sexual tension was INTENSE and I LOVED IT! Am I using "LOVE" a lot? Maybe, but it's just me being honest. I think McLean is an epic writer. I was highlighting almost every page, I could quote the whole read. I loved More Than This. <br><br><br><b>I was absorbed, I laughed, I cried, I was gutted and I SWOONED VERY HARD.</b><br><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/1lMRZZ2" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430518i/863146._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>THIS IS AN ABSOLUTE READ.<br><br><br>5 STARS</b><br><br><br>Oh and I can't wait for book 2, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/686480872" rel="nofollow noopener">More Than Her</a>. More Than This does not end on a cliffy (Thank You), but you get an intro to More Than Her and oh gosh, I just want this read .... so BAD.<br><br><br>Okay, enough of me gushing, go read More Than This and then message me so we can talk about it.<br><br><i>An ARC was provided by the author in exchange for an honest review</i><br></span>

<div id="review_1280422691" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1280422691" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1280422691?book_show_action=true">May 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to • Lisa • by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites">Alexis *Reality Bites*</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1280422691" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16026225870656873638"><b>FOUR MORE THAN STARS.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>I think I'm in love with this beautifully broken girl.</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431691839i/14860261._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Why, oh why, oh why, did I wait so long to start this series? It's been under my nose for so long, so many of my friends have read, devoured and adored this series and here I am only just starting this epic 'more than' marathon. I can only say that I'm an idiot, but at least right now I'm a happy idiot and blissfully enjoying the start of my Jay McLean type book binge. From prologue to epilogue this book had me wrappe</span>
  <span id="freeText16026225870656873638" style="display:none"><b>FOUR MORE THAN STARS.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>I think I'm in love with this beautifully broken girl.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431691839i/14860261._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Why, oh why, oh why, did I wait so long to start this series? It's been under my nose for so long, so many of my friends have read, devoured and adored this series and here I am only just starting this epic 'more than' marathon. I can only say that I'm an idiot, but at least right now I'm a happy idiot and blissfully enjoying the start of my Jay McLean type book binge. From prologue to epilogue this book had me wrapped round it's little finger and I'm happy for all you Jay McLean enthusiasts to sit back and give me a big smug 'told you so'. There wasn't much not to love about this author and her writing style, I for one feel hooked and I'm hoping to love the rest of the series just as much, (if not more).<br><br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>Jay McLean books are definitely shaping up to be paperback worthy treasures. Just look at those covers, they totally appeal to my cover lust addiction and what's truly making me break out in the book addict happy dance is the fact that what's inside the front cover is gorgeously lovely too (day made). 'More than this' is a book that has that unforgettable quality about it, the author has certainly written a story with some 'wow' moments and it definitely had some plot twists that I honestly did not see coming. The book spoke to me of friendships, love, healing, heart ache, pain and belonging. It was a journey that I loved and even though I'm super late to the party I'm glad I finally decided to take the plunge and start this series. And what a beginning it was, I don't know whether to love the slow burn nature of this story telling more or Jake Andrews the sweetest new adult hero to ever be created. Almost read in one sitting I was helpless to this authors writing charms, if I was to say I had one regret it was not starting this series sooner, I feel like I have missed out on all the love and excitement surrounding this series but I'm more than willing to make up for time now and I'm gagging to get started on Logan's story in book two of the series 'More than her'. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431691839i/14860262._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Why not five?</b><br>For those of you who are interested (and even if you're not, just humour me) when I rate a book I don't rate in halves, so if a book falls somewhere in between a star rating I always round down. So what I'm trying to explain (rather badly) is that this book fell somewhere between a four and a five but something held me back from giving out the full out five. And why? Well I don't want to start being nick picky about a book that quite frankly will be unforgettable but I did have a few niggles that made me want to hold off from a five star. Simply put I needed some more insight into the journey of the characters, I wanted to get into their heads a little more and understand some of the decision making and feelings. I also found myself wondering about certain plot lines and questioning just odd bits and bobs. One of the things I loved about this book was confusingly one of the things that slightly annoyed me and that my fellow readers was the whip lash, and the non communication about how we really feel about each other drama and The see-saw playground love adventure that had me going round and round in circles with this couple. However, with those gripes aside this book has owned me and I don't want to dwell on the pitfalls so much as what I did love and I'm sure that overall this is going to be a five star series for my book tastes. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431691839i/14860263._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>If like me, you find yourself being a book idiot too, and you haven't yet started this series then quite frankly I have nothing else to say to you than this; you must, must, must start this series right about now (I demand it). And if you are a fellow addict that has already loved this series, then I'm proud to say I'm giddy exited to have finally joined team McLean. (See what I did there)? I read a lot of books in the romance genre and I love everything about this book community and the special ability that these authors have to give me an escape from reality, but what made this book stand out to me was it's heart grabbing originality and honest sentiment. I really could not be any happier than I am right now, as well as this book taking me out of a reading rut, I've also managed to discover a new author to love and a series that I can't wait to read the rest of (this is officially a happy book day). That's it from me and with nothing more to say, fingers crossed to loving book two in the series ... </span>
  <a data-text-id="16026225870656873638" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<div id="review_1105104501" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1105104501" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1105104501?book_show_action=true">Nov 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Beverly by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1105104501" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5049235854451141553"><b>This is a <i>read now</i> on NetGalley - if you haven't fallen in love with this series, now is your chance!!</b><br/><br/><b>5 <i>More than love this series</i> Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416267026i/11925335._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This series was recommended to me a while back by two of my favorite friends, and every week I kept moving it on my calendar. Well this last week I decided to read some of the books that I have been meaning to read, but they kept getting pushed back. I knew I had to start with this one, and let me tell you I am so glad! I have joked I am the last person on GR to</span>
  <span id="freeText5049235854451141553" style="display:none"><b>This is a <i>read now</i> on NetGalley - if you haven't fallen in love with this series, now is your chance!!</b><br><br><b>5 <i>More than love this series</i> Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416267026i/11925335._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This series was recommended to me a while back by two of my favorite friends, and every week I kept moving it on my calendar. Well this last week I decided to read some of the books that I have been meaning to read, but they kept getting pushed back. I knew I had to start with this one, and let me tell you I am so glad! I have joked I am the last person on GR to read this series and that is probably true, but if you like me have not read this series yet JUST DO IT!!<br><br>When the story starts we meet Mikayla. She is the smart girl, dating the popular jock and best friends with the head cheerleader. She doesn’t really feel like that make sense, but it has been her life for the last four years. On prom night her senior year her entire world comes crashing down around her. <br><br>The one positive outcome from that night is she meet Jake Andrews. Jake Andrews is kind of a <i>big deal</i>, he is a star baseball player, already being scouted my major league scouts. Kayla and Jake meet and from the that moment they have this connection. Events bring them even more closer together and gradually things progress. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416267026i/11925336._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As always I don’t want to give anything away, because I think the less you know going into a book the better off you are. This book has a lot of shocking moments and I wasn’t aware any of it was going to take place, and loved it even more. <br><br>What you need to know is this book is absolutely beautiful and it will quickly hook you, and have you wanting to read the rest as soon as possible. The connection Mikayla and Jake share is beautifully heartbreaking.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I think I am in love with this beautifully broken girl.”</i>
</b><br><br>I loved seeing the character development and growth. I loved how things weren’t cookie cutter, but more realistic. I love how Kayla wanted to be more before things could progress, and I loved how Jake was patient and consistent. I have read so many books this year and this series is definitely a favorite. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416267026i/11925337._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>"He’s my Jake and I’m his Kayla."</i>
</b></span>
