    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_673291720" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/673291720" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/673291720?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer673291720" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14141037374477048609"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429989i/861838._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED **<br/><br/><i>
  <b>"In one night my fairytale ended. Or it may have begun..."</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>More Than This </i> was a very sweet and sometimes heartbreaking book about love, loss, healing and friendship. It was laced with some sadness following a horrific tragedy but the feeling of the book was more focused on healing, rebuilding and finding happiness again.<br/><br/>I loved the hero and the core group of characters and will be looking forward to the next in the series. This one however reads a complete standal</span>
  <span id="freeText14141037374477048609" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429989i/861838._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED **<br><br><i>
  <b>"In one night my fairytale ended. Or it may have begun..."</b>
</i><br><br><i>More Than This </i> was a very sweet and sometimes heartbreaking book about love, loss, healing and friendship. It was laced with some sadness following a horrific tragedy but the feeling of the book was more focused on healing, rebuilding and finding happiness again.<br><br>I loved the hero and the core group of characters and will be looking forward to the next in the series. This one however reads a complete standalone with a happy ending :)<br><br>So, about the book...<br><br>Mikayla's life fell apart the night her boyfriend of four years cheated on her. On the same night, she met Jake. Having witnessed the whole debacle and seen how deeply she was hurting, Jake felt innately protective of her and invited her to come join him and his friends. Something about him just felt 'right' and she trusted him enough to accept. His friends welcomed and acceptd her and for a few hours, she was able to feel happy again.<br><br>Everything was beginning to pick up until they returned home and her entire world was shattered by a senseless tragedy that wiped away everything she loved in life in one horrific moment.<br><br>But she wasn't alone. Jake took her in and this boy who she'd known for less than a day became her pillar of support and source of comfort.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I fell asleep in Jake's arms, sheltered from all the bad and evil in the world."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>It was so heartwarming to see how supportive and kind Jake's family was to her. Not to mention the fact that there was definitely <em>more</em> between Mikayla and Jake. You could feel it, and they knew it but given the tragedy, their feelings were put on on hold while she healed. There were no labels, nothing official, but their hearts bonded. Jake was there for her every step of the way and their romance developed very slowly and naturally.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"She's just, more than anyone else. We haven't slept together, we haven't even kissed, and she's just ... more."</em>
</blockquote><br>Here they were, at 18 years old, facing a horrible tragedy and yet also falling in love. They really held back on acting on on their feelings for a while and I understood that. Jake was giving her time to grieve and Mikayla needed to to just heal and also felt like she had to stand on her own before she could fully allow herself to fall in love. I understood where she was coming from but this aspect did lead to some frustration later on in the story.<br><br>I really have to say that Jake was just amazing. I loved him! Between his slight accent and deep voice (which I <em>so</em> wish I could hear) mixed in with both his naturally protective vibe and his sweet gentlemanly side too, he was just some kind of perfect. He loved her, was patient, kind, thoughtful, understanding... everything about him made him very easy to swoon over :)<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"I saw more than a few guys checking her out. I couldn't help putting my arm around her, and bringing her into me. Because it's the stone age and I'm a caveman."</em>
</blockquote><br>I liked Mikayla. She was a bookworm too and I mean, she knew who Josh Bennett was, okay? *grins* I did really like her but I had a little harder time fully connecting with her as the book progressed because of they way she kept Jake at bay for so long. I will say though, that her feelings and reasons <em>were</em> all fully explained in the end so I could definitely see her side of the story. And apart from that one thing, I really liked her as a character and loved her and Jake together.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Do not settle for anything less than the Jake Andrews of the world. Because they exist, and not just in fairytales."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>The supporting characters in this book are wonderful! I loved them! Jake's friends were just awesome! Their group dynamic was so much fun to read about and I felt instantly connected to them. I loved how easily they accepted Mikayla into their group as well with no questions. And some of the couples were just adorable. Check out this quote about one of the guys, it makes me want to read a whole book about him:<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"He's not the hearts and flowers kind of guy, but he's the heart and soul kind, and fuck if every girl would rather that than the flowers."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>And this book officially has the coolest book parents of all time. I really loved seeing parents depicted this way in a book because, not to say that it's the norm, but many books have rather troubled parental relations and seeing a family that was a genuine unit who loved each other, and were understanding and supportive was a welcome change.<br><br>We're told the story in alternating POV's and so we do get the complete picture here. It was a very easy book to read and the pages flew by quickly. I found the story jumped around a little bit more than I'd like but there were no slow points and that the story line was constantly moving forward.<br><br>For some reason, I really expected this book to be heavy and intense and, don't get me wrong, there were certainly places of sadness but it also had a lot of lighter, funny moments that shone though.<br><br>While I loved that in the beginning nothing was rushed, I did feel like they (well, Mikayla) held back for a little longer than I'd have wanted. I just felt bad for Jake - he was just crazily, head over heels falling for this girl who kept holding a huge part of herself back.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <strong>
      <em>"It's the fucking hardest thing to do, to be around the person you love, with everything you have, and not be able to love them."</em>
    </strong>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>That being said, there was never any doubt in my mind or their hearts that they were meant to be.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"It’s just you. It’s only ever been just you. It will always only ever be just you."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>One little tiny thing that bothered me was that I felt like despite the fact that they were in high school, some of the slang was a little over used - like 'legit'. But it's a small complaint.<br><br>The story was addictive in the sense of I really could have easily read it in one sitting had my time allowed for it. It kind of rode the line between YA and NA. There were some very steamy scenes but no actual descriptive sex.<br><br>I wanted a little 'more' some places and a little 'less' in others but I still really enjoyed the story, really loved Jake and Mikayla as a couple and am glad I read it.<br><br>The next book will be about Jake's best friend and so while I'm sure we may see these characters in it, this book fully reads as a standalone with a happy ending (complete with an epilogue too!) so if you like the sound of this one, you're safe to start it whenever you wish :)<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <strong>
      <em>"I so much more than a lot like you."</em>
    </strong>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br>4 stars.<br><br>For now, here's my casting for Jake:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429989i/861839._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1375710763l/18285151.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> *Mikayla*<br>In one night my fairytale ended. Or it may have begun. This is my story of friendship and love, heartbreak and desire, and the strength to show weakness.<br><br>*Jake*<br>One night I met a girl. A sad and broken girl, but one more beautiful than any other. She laughed through her sadness, while I loved through her heartbreak.<br><br>*This is our story of a maybe ever after.* </i><br><br>*****************************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14141037374477048609" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_666946648" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/666946648?book_show_action=true">Jul 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie">Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer666946648" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5461380656612323279"><b>4 So Much More Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381553464i/5020432.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Mikayla has everything going for her. A loving family, a hot boyfriend and a best friend, it seems nothing could happen to ruin the life she's living. Until the night of her prom when everything falls apart, everything she's always held dear ripped from her life. Everything she has always believed in is proved to have been a lie.<br/><br/>The one thing that anchors her and prevents her from drifting away is Jake. A chance meeting but he becomes her saving grace, the one who pulls her o</span>
  <span id="freeText5461380656612323279" style="display:none"><b>4 So Much More Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381553464i/5020432.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mikayla has everything going for her. A loving family, a hot boyfriend and a best friend, it seems nothing could happen to ruin the life she's living. Until the night of her prom when everything falls apart, everything she's always held dear ripped from her life. Everything she has always believed in is proved to have been a lie.<br><br>The one thing that anchors her and prevents her from drifting away is Jake. A chance meeting but he becomes her saving grace, the one who pulls her out of the darkness threatening to swallow her whole. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381563583i/5037293.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381571380i/5051254.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Before meeting Kayla, Jake had only one goal in mind. Starting his career in sports. Nothing has ever distracted has ever meant more than this, until Mikayla comes into his life. He wants her badly and is prepared to wait as long as she needs, he's protective of her, doesn't want to see her hurt.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381571380i/5051255.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their relationship is tentative at first, but as time goes by the begin to have deeper feelings for each other. Mikayla's traumatic experience is all that stands in their way. It's up to Jake to show her that he can help her, that pushing him away is the worst thing she could do. He has to prove how much he loves her flaws and all, that by being together she can heal.<br><br><u>
  <b>Final Thoughts</b>
</u><br>I genuinely enjoyed this book. I loved Jake, he was the perfect blend of sweetness and alpha male. He never gave up on Mikayla. I liked Mikayla too, although her logic was a bit exasperating at times, but it was understandable, seeing as she had gone through something traumatic. The dialogue between the characters and writing was very realistic making this book very engaging so I was never bored. The angst wasn't over done so I didn't feel overwhelmed which makes it a great read in my opinion.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2529952339" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2453215255608076363">This is the first new adult novel I’ve ever read (listened to on an audiobook). At first, I thought I was reading YA. I read probably one YA a year now that I’m no longer in junior high, which was one million years ago. Then when there was all this explicit sex and swearing, I thought, my my, YA has changed.<br/><br/>Duh. New adult. I’d heard the term, I’d just never stumbled on it before. <br/><br/>The premise of the novel starts out well. Mikayla goes to prom with high hopes, only to be betrayed not just by her l</span>
  <span id="freeText2453215255608076363" style="display:none">This is the first new adult novel I’ve ever read (listened to on an audiobook). At first, I thought I was reading YA. I read probably one YA a year now that I’m no longer in junior high, which was one million years ago. Then when there was all this explicit sex and swearing, I thought, my my, YA has changed.<br /><br />Duh. New adult. I’d heard the term, I’d just never stumbled on it before. <br /><br />The premise of the novel starts out well. Mikayla goes to prom with high hopes, only to be betrayed not just by her long-time boyfriend but her best friend. Jake witnesses the drama and does his best to emotionally help Kayla. Except what seems like the worst night of her life gets much, much worse. <br /><br />I liked both lead characters. Jake falls in love with Kayla and expresses it by being as supportive as possible. <br /><br />Maybe because I listened to it instead of reading it, I kept getting confused by the many high school characters and the “romances” (hook-ups) and drama of teenage life. <br /><br />I think this is probably a well-done novel for the genre. It just turns out it’s the kind of novel I want to read.<br /><br />For more reviews, please visit: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.theresaalan.net/blog">http://www.theresaalan.net/blog</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2453215255608076363" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

The kind of love that never ends!!! <br>The kind of love that from the first moment stand by you and become more that everything!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431275ra/865311.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yeah, it was a messy situation but it was as α result of a disastrous beginning!!!<br>Did i confuse you??? Let me make the things clear for you...<br><br>Mikayla is living a nice life... She is having the most lovely parents and a little young sister that she loves very much!!! They are a very happy family!!! She is dating James for four years now and she is having an amazing best friend, Megan... <br>Oh, yeah! I know! She is so lucky!!! <br>Until an asshole spills his drink on her dress in the prom night!!!! <br>Yeah, i know... Who cares about this shit???? Nobody else is there for her... <br>So, between them forms a strange and deep bond that they lead them in new and unknown paths!!!<br><br>I felt so pity for Kayla...       <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1037082025" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2735065259249492559"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505117282i/23884638._SX540_.jpg' alt='4-5-stars.png (651×165)' width='222' height='56' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It's no secret that Jay Mclean is one of my all time favorite mf authors. I have read all the books in this series and the spin off and I keep re-reading them, because they are like comfort-food to me. Some I love more than others, but I really enjoyed each and every one.<br/><br/>This first book is Jake and Kayla's story and though it's not my favorite in this series (those rights go to Cam and Lucy), it's still very good. I would also recommend reading this series in order and coming from me (who reads </span>
  <span id="freeText2735065259249492559" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505117282i/23884638._SX540_.jpg" alt="4-5-stars.png (651×165)" width="222" height="56" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's no secret that Jay Mclean is one of my all time favorite mf authors. I have read all the books in this series and the spin off and I keep re-reading them, because they are like comfort-food to me. Some I love more than others, but I really enjoyed each and every one.<br><br>This first book is Jake and Kayla's story and though it's not my favorite in this series (those rights go to Cam and Lucy), it's still very good. I would also recommend reading this series in order and coming from me (who reads everything ass backwards), that's saying something ;)<br><br>Your life can change in the blink of an eye.... which is exactly what happend to Kayla.<br><br>Kayla is an sweet girl. Her life is pretty great, she has some good friends and she is dating the school's popular jock. She is about to go to prom and have the night of her life....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505117282i/23884639._SX540_.jpg" alt="Cute Girl Wallpapers HD Free Download." width="283" height="159" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In just one night her whole life gets turned around. Her prom-night isn't going the way she expected, but little does she know, that things are about get much much worse....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494924871ra/22766210.gif" alt="tumblr_inline_nshha5J5l01s3t5ed_500.gif (250×278)" width="181" height="201" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The only light shining on this devastating day is Jake, ....the handsome star baseball player from another school, whom met earlier that day. He becomes a rock for her to lean on... when all else is gone.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1505117282ra/23884640.gif" alt="light-gif-3.gif (500×334)" width="270" height="180" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He is patient and sweet and slowly he starts to heal Kayla's broken heart.<br><br>This books opens with utter devastation.... but I closed it with a huge smile on my face. I loved all the characters in this book. Jake was awesome and his friends are the bomb !!<br><br>I loved seeing Kayla heal slowly and how they went from friends to lovers.... The sexual tension in this book almost killed me and there were times I just wanted to yell at them, to get it on already ... which thankfully they do :P<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1505117282i/23884641._SY540_.jpg" alt="28031a6c0dd807caeba54aaf0aad0c82.jpg (367×550)" width="234" height="351" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><em>
  <strong>“I’m your Jake,” he smiles. “And you’re my Kayla.” </strong>
</em><br><br>I highly recommend this series to everyone... each book just gets better and better and I can honestly say, that book 4 in this series <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18628601-more-than-forever" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">"More Than Forever"</a> , is one of my all time favorite mf books !! First you gotta read about Logan (book 2/3) though... Cause who would want to skip Logan's book ;)<br><br> <br> </span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18159498072024603869">I had no idea what I was getting into when I picked this book out. It was on KU, so I thought... why not?<br/><br/>I more than really really liked this book. More than really liked Kayla and I for sure really really more than liked Jake. <br/><br/>More Than This was absolutely wonderful and heartbreaking. It is about high school/ college kids but the story is amazing. <br/><br/>Now I'm on to Logan's story!</span>

<div id="review_687650977" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/687650977" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/687650977?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18129149-more-than-this">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">NA readers, lovers of angst and drama</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Duchess Nicole by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites">Alexis *Reality Bites*</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=4-star-read">4-star-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=hyped">hyped</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-new-adult">genre-new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer687650977" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3268637906542258192"><b>
  <blockquote>"Talking without speaking. Feeling without touching."</blockquote>
</b><br/>I shouldn't like this book, but I really did. I've had all these issues with this genre lately, but I keep getting sucked into reading them. And sure, yeah...this story contained some of my pet peeves. It's pretty darn angsty. The setup is a bit off the charts, and so is the melodrama. <i>But I was glued to these pages.</i> <br/><br/>I don't want to even say what happens within the first few chapters because I think it would spoil the story. I went into it</span>
  <span id="freeText3268637906542258192" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>"Talking without speaking. Feeling without touching."</blockquote>
</b><br>I shouldn't like this book, but I really did. I've had all these issues with this genre lately, but I keep getting sucked into reading them. And sure, yeah...this story contained some of my pet peeves. It's pretty darn angsty. The setup is a bit off the charts, and so is the melodrama. <i>But I was glued to these pages.</i> <br><br>I don't want to even say what happens within the first few chapters because I think it would spoil the story. I went into it with only a vague idea of what to expect, and I'm glad. <br><br><b>
  <u>WHAT WORKED:</u>
</b><br>I loved JAKE!!!! I know, I know...everyone loves Jake. But seriously, this guy is amazing! He's got that super protective, gentle air. He's attracted to Kayla (Mackayla, Mickey) instantly. When he witnesses the ultimate betrayal, his protective instincts kick in, and he's there to comfort her. He's her shoulder to cry on, her big strong man to rely on.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"I think I'm in love with this beautifully broken girl."</blockquote>
</b> <br><br>Perfect word to describe Jake: Steadfast!!<br><br>So not only is he the biggest freaking sweetheart ever, he's also a major hottie. Here's our boy...and oh, look! There are his group of cohorts in the background...I'm seeing the guy in back as Logan...<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432039i/867570._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love how Jake says...in such a self deprecating manner...<b>"I'm kind of a <i>big deal."</i></b> What a cutie!!!<br><br>There was a lot of funny in this book, which I didn't expect with all of the sad subject matter. Let's face it: Kayla goes through some really horrific times within the six or so months that this book takes place. But there a moments of much needed humor to lighten the feel.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"His eyes bug out of his head. "Okay, smartass," he yells, but it comes out 'smuuhtuhhs.' Australians don't use R's apparently..."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Oh, yeah...that Australian accent...freaking YUM!!!<br><br>I also adore it when the author makes it apparent that she also is an avid reader, that she also has book boyfriends, and that she might actually obsess over them just like we do. I mean, what better way to make your readers identify with your characters than do mimic their insanity? Perfection. Shout out to Josh Bennett from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16151178.The_Sea_of_Tranquility" title="The Sea of Tranquility by Katja Millay" rel="nofollow noopener">The Sea of Tranquility</a><br><br>I loved all of the secondary characters...Jake's group of friends really were so wonderful. They instantly accepted Mickey(Kayla) into the fold, and added more of that humor to the mix, but also gave Mickey the loyalty that she didn't get from those that should have been loyal at the beginning. Here's a tidbit from Lucy, the most awesome of drunks:<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"...that fucking bitch has it all, ten out of ten every fucking thing. She's super smart. Like, fucking Harvard smart. She's nice to fucking everybody. She's always looked like the cover of a fucking magazine and I hate it so much and if I could get away with it I'd fucking cut a bitch for you."</blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>
  <u>WHAT DIDN'T WORK:</u>
</b><br>The whole back and forth between Jake and Kayla, the jealousy, the things so typical to this genre that drive me freaking batty. I mean, seriously...the dude has practically carried you through the last few months of your life...it's okay if he talks to a girl. The whole no-kissing situation started off as cute, but it eventually bugged that ever loving crap out of me. It's just too unbelievable, and with all of the other sexual things they did, not kissing seemed like an odd plot device. <br><br>Also, this entire book is one HUGE TURN ON................<br><b>Every...<br>Freaking...<br>Page...<br>Is...<br>Foreplay.</b><br><br>So that "sex" scene? <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380432039i/867571.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Left me hanging, big time. In fact, I'm not sure...did they even actually have sex? Hmmm...very disappointing. If your going to make the book THAT sexual in nature...and let's face it...this book is extremely sexual....PLEASE, for the love of God...give us some real sex. It doesn't have to be explicit but come on...<br><br>Wrapping it up...I really loved this book, sort of despite myself...these characters are all normal people...no one really acts over the top or out of character for the way they were intended. Yes, it's a bit too dramatic, but I've just resigned myself to a bit of soap opera with this genre. I remember being a teenager, and a young adult. This is pretty much the way I felt about everything...emotions running amuck and all that.<br><br>I see that there is another book in the works about Logan, which I'm sure we're all stoked about, especially after showing his sweetheart side to Mickey a couple of times and spouting his drunken longing for love. He hasn't found a girl that makes him <i>feel</i>? I bet Jay McLean can!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3268637906542258192" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/734924890?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>

Here's the link: <a href='http://www.jaymcleanauthor.com/jakyalabonus' rel='nofollow noopener'>click here</a><br/><br/><b> 5 stars!!!<br/><br/>I loved this book so, so much I am going to do an interview as a review!!! First time so bear with me! All answers are from the book and not made up! I promise there are NO SPOILERS! Okay here we go! </b><br/><br/><b>Me</b>: Hi Ms. Jones! Thanks for agreeing to meet with me! (Technically, I had to drag her here…prying her away from Jake was nearly impossible)<br/><br/><b>Mikayla:</b> Micky.</span>
  <span id="freeText9144255377532071158" style="display:none"><u>UPDATE:</u> Jay has released an EXTRA bonus scene 10/10/2013! It'll be spoiler-y if you haven't read the book. Here's the link: <a href="http://www.jaymcleanauthor.com/jakyalabonus" rel="nofollow noopener">click here</a><br /><br /><b> 5 stars!!!<br /><br />I loved this book so, so much I am going to do an interview as a review!!! First time so bear with me! All answers are from the book and not made up! I promise there are NO SPOILERS! Okay here we go! </b><br /><br /><b>Me</b>: Hi Ms. Jones! Thanks for agreeing to meet with me! (Technically, I had to drag her here…prying her away from Jake was nearly impossible)<br /><br /><b>Mikayla:</b> Micky...call me Micky...please. <br /><br /><b>Me</b>: Okay Micky! *clears throat* I know you’ve heard this many times in the book, but I am so, so sorry for that night. I just…just can’t imagine what you must have felt. What you still feel.<br /><br /><b>Mikayla</b>: *her eyes are brimming with unshed tears* It was one night. One night when everything changed. It was so much more than just the betrayal. It was the tragedy. The deaths. The murders. But it was also that feeling. That feeling of falling. <br /><br /><b>Me</b>: *opens and closes mouth…I mean, what can you say to that?* Wow, what an eloquent way of describing a tragic night. Micky, I…wait, feeling of falling? Falling deeper into a pit? Or falling in love with….<br /><br /><b>Mikayla</b>: *blank stare, no answer*<br /><br /><b>Me</b>: Okaaaay then, I take that as “read the book to find out.” *mutters* Micky, what was you reaction when you first saw Jake, um, after that <i>incident</i>?<br /><br /><b>Mikayla</b>: I can’t believe <i>accent boy</i> just witnessed that whole thing. I’m so fricken embarrassed by all of it. Mainly because I was the dumb girl that just got played for <i>so</i> long. <br /><br /><b>Me</b>: Yes…Believe me if I was there, my first move would be to bash a certain someone’s nuts. He completely deserved it. Moving along, how is Jake’s family? They certainly played a huge role in your life and in the book. Just curious to know how you’re taking it all in…<br /><br /><b>Mikayla</b>: It hurts less today then it did yesterday. Because being here, being with them, it’s familiar in a good way…Jake, he makes things hurt a little less. He…he’s <i>home</i> for me right now. He’s <i>my Jake.</i> And I’m <i>his</i> Kayla. <br /><br /><b>Me</b>: *sniffle* Oh yes, I understand. *romantic sigh* (Is it just me, or did the air get really heavy in here??) Oh Micky!!! I have to ask this question!! I absolutely ADORE Lucy! She’s literally my favorite character, well, after you hehe. What’s your most memorable impression of her? Care to share?<br /><br /><b>Mikayla</b>: “I swear to god, Micky. I’ll cut a bitch for you, just let me go, Cam. Let me go!” *snickers*<br /><br /><b>Me</b>: *laughs* Oh, I so remember that scene! That chick cracks me up! And she reads! What an awesome buddy! I’d love a Lucy in my life, especially a drunk one! Okay, as we are winding down, I have the most serious question to ask you, and I'm not the only one who wants an answer. Are you ready?<br /><br />***Pause***<br /><br />If you could describe Jake in one sentence, what would you say? *leans forward to hear answer*<br /><br /><b>Mikayla</b>: I feel sorry for all the girls in the world that never get to experience a Jake Andrews at least once in their lifetime.<br /><br /><b>Me</b>: HOLY. SHIT. Me too...*plotting a character kidnapping* If only I had one of those…*wink* Well, thank you so much Micky! I’m so glad I got a chance to speak with you!<br /><br /><b>Mikayla</b>: Okay then, thank you!<br /><br /><b>Me</b>: AAAAAAND CUT! *turns to you* Thanks for being part of the audience! I hope you enjoyed listening to Micky as much as I did! <br /><br /><u>
  <b>Thoughts the second time I read it</b>
</u><br /><br />I read this first in August and can I say WOW! I’ve highlighted pages and pages of epic quotes and all I did was just look at them and –boom – I’d remember <i>exactly</i> what the scene was or what the characters were doing. Like the first time I read it, this book grabbed me by the collar and dragged me in until I finished! <b>Could. Not. Put. Down.</b> So don’t even try to read it unless you’re prepared to finish it in one sitting! Jay McLean, you are my hero! Cannot wait for Logan’s story! </span>

<div id="review_666897601" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/666897601" />
    <a title="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3758447-vikki-squee-lite"><img alt="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368215503p2/3758447.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/666897601?book_show_action=true">Jul 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~" href="/user/show/3758447-vikki-squee-lite">Vikki ~ *squee* lite ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18129149-more-than-this">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=sweet">sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=sniffle">sniffle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=awesome-sauce">awesome-sauce</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=swoon">swoon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=new-ya">new-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3758447-vikki-squee-lite?shelf=i-didn-t-see-that-coming">i-didn-t-see-that-coming</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer666897601" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4641148773365093686"><br/> <br/>I adored this book. I loved every single second (even the frustrating ones). <br/><br/>At its heart, this was a modern day fairytale about a “regular” girl. And, as all good fairytales do, it starts with a tragedy. Well, actually two tragedies. The first is the catalyst for Mikayla and Jake’s chance meeting. The second is what both keeps them together, and threatens to tear them apart.<br/><br/><a href='http://s50.photobucket.com/albums/f339/vikkimathews/?action=view&current=c1fbad57f8c7d2758dfd3e2b2514f4ae_zpscc5ce0dc.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429075i/859176._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>The thing that makes this story different, and sets it apart from the hundreds of other NA books I’ve read with simil</span>
  <span id="freeText4641148773365093686" style="display:none"><br> <br>I adored this book. I loved every single second (even the frustrating ones). <br><br>At its heart, this was a modern day fairytale about a “regular” girl. And, as all good fairytales do, it starts with a tragedy. Well, actually two tragedies. The first is the catalyst for Mikayla and Jake’s chance meeting. The second is what both keeps them together, and threatens to tear them apart.<br><br><a href="http://s50.photobucket.com/albums/f339/vikkimathews/?action=view&amp;current=c1fbad57f8c7d2758dfd3e2b2514f4ae_zpscc5ce0dc.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429075i/859176._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>The thing that makes this story different, and sets it apart from the hundreds of other NA books I’ve read with similar themes, is all in the execution.<br>There was this amazing mix of humor and sweetness amidst the sadness, lust and swooning. It just struck the perfect balance for me. <br><br>I cannot imagine a more perfect hero then Jake. (Except that he’s not perfect, just almost perfect – which of course, made him really perfect) He truly was a hero in this book. He is sweet, understanding, protective, and all around swoon-worthy. He was also a guy. His inner dialogue had me laughing more than once.<br><br><b>
  <i> “Nothing says awkward like coming in your pants while dry humping.” </i>
</b><br><br> I loved how he took care of Kayla, and how basically from the moment they met, he was willing to do whatever it took for her to be ok.<br><br>I appreciated how their relationship developed (even if I wanted to scream with frustration a few times). While they bonded quickly, neither of them was willing to rush into something, though they both had different reasons for that. <br>I think that a lack of communication was the one thing that irked me ever so slightly. (ok, maybe more than slightly). <br><br>The story is told in dual POV, so we get to see what both Mikayla and Jake are thinking. This is both wonderful, and frustrating, because as the reader, we KNOW how much they love each other, but neither of them is willing to put the words out there. There is always talk of “show don’t tell” – but Mikayla and Jake took that to a whole new level. They “showed” so much that there was so doubt in anyone’s mind how they felt about each other, but the lack of “tell” created some serious problems. I have to say, I do lay the blame for that more on Jake then Mikayla. You know why she’s not “telling”, and while it was unnecessary, I understood and sympathized with where she was coming from. I had to keep reminding myself that they were only 18, so I didn’t try and climb in the book and shake some sense into them. But, in the end, I loved them. Even when I wanted to kill them. I was so invested in their story – in <i>them</i> that every threat to their relationship had my heart pounding. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ near the end, when Jake finally lashed out, and Mikayla couldn’t tell him what he wanted to hear, I swear my heart actually broke  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://s50.photobucket.com/albums/f339/vikkimathews/?action=view&amp;current=93b228df77080d723370e510c5cbc72d_zpsf78835d7.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429075i/859177._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>The cast of secondary characters were amazing. I absolutely loved all of them. Cam and “book-worm” Lucy, Heidi and Dylan, and Logan all brought so much color and humor to a story that could have gotten bogged down with the heavy topics (and seemingly never ending sexual frustration). I can’t imagine anyone NOT wishing for a group of friends just like them. Lucy in particular was a favorite of mine. I always have a soft spot for fellow book lovers (even if they are fictional characters). Drunk Lucy was even more fun.<br><br><i>
  <b>”I swear to god, Micky,” Lucy snarls at her, Cam’s pretending to hold her back, amused by her drunk state. “I’ll cut a bitch for you, just let me go, Cam. Let me go!” she yells, trying to fight his grip. </b>
</i><br><br>Overall, it was a beautiful story, wonderfully told – that is immediately getting a space on my favorites shelf. Highly recommended. <br> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="4641148773365093686" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText16753200714269262499" style="display:none">4.5--<b>SWEET and HEART-WARMING</b>--Stars!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380303130ra/687727.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That was the sweetest story ever! *sigh* <br><br>Mikayla's life changes forever the night of her prom.     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1128196766" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1128196766" />
    <a title="Claire Robinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14026987-claire-robinson"><img alt="Claire Robinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431471072p2/14026987.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1128196766?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Claire Robinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Claire Robinson" href="/user/show/14026987-claire-robinson">Claire Robinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781477820384" href="/book/show/22877448-more-than-this">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14026987-claire-robinson?shelf=shit-hot-series">shit-hot-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1128196766" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13294876138284178967">4.5 - <b>There is only so much shit I can take before all the fucked-up things in my life consume me.</b> Stars!<br/><br/><i>More Than this</i> is the first book I have read by Jay McLean, it is what I affectionately class as a <i>‘kitchen sinker’</i>, in that it feels like the author has literally thrown as many tropes as she possibly can at it. This is the type of book I need to be in a certain mood for, otherwise I just get frustrated and annoyed. <br/><br/>Luckily, I was in the right mood, although I did get a little frustrated, bu</span>
  <span id="freeText13294876138284178967" style="display:none">4.5 - <b>There is only so much shit I can take before all the fucked-up things in my life consume me.</b> Stars!<br><br><i>More Than this</i> is the first book I have read by Jay McLean, it is what I affectionately class as a <i>‘kitchen sinker’</i>, in that it feels like the author has literally thrown as many tropes as she possibly can at it. This is the type of book I need to be in a certain mood for, otherwise I just get frustrated and annoyed. <br><br>Luckily, I was in the right mood, although I did get a little frustrated, but that was more to do with the copious amounts of almost home-runs, and dry (as well as wet) non-humping that went on for most of this book.<br><br><b>I’ve been a part of the worst night of her life.</b><br><br>Mikayla has to be one of the unluckiest characters I have had the opportunity of reading about in quite a while. It is difficult to write a detailed review because of her story as it would pretty much give most of the book away. Betrayal and Tragedy are words that are used in the synopsis, and they do pretty much sum up the biggest parts of the story.<br><br>Jake and his friends are what made this book for me, I liked Kayla for the most part, and even though the bulk of the story is a result of the things that happen to her, he was the one I actually cared about as the book progressed. The guy (as well as his family and friends) literally puts his life on-hold to help her through the worst times imaginable, and at points I really struggled to understand her actions and reactions towards him. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421063478i/13317278.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What dropped this book from the full 5 stars for me was the fact that with all the drama already going on the author then felt the need to add in random acts of both of them trying to make the other jealous as well as failing to communicate with each other about totally banal things bringing about totally pointless arguments as well. I also found the whole ‘Casey interludes’ to be a complete waste of time (unless she figures in other books in the series more prominently, if so I will take that point back!).<br><br><b>”It’s just you. It’s only ever been just you. It will always only ever be just you.”</b><br><br>I am late to the party with this series, but I kind of like that, because I now have 3 books I can read in succession and a new release due at some point in 2015. Win-Win! This may have been the first book I have read by this author; it damn sure won’t be the last.<br><br>ARC generously provided via Netgalley, in exchange for the above honest review.<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13294876138284178967" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FqAvKsjuWkw/Xr/fh/+IVhtDiuMKdmy2Bi1NRAWlqNafFTb5UUrFbBnyxv2pUtC3czfDRq5UD45vw54CqIrXow==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RikgCdjVNJlT2Qmnq4TJgZpoy5vOm/j3O9Zgo5gzbbfPnDnaQXGruXV1cIWFKZFg8hyCPmq5m89SOLPlNRwSwg==')})
  }
//]]>
